<P class="p40 ft29"><SPAN class="ft29">(6)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft35">‚ÄúIrtibat Kurulusu‚Äù bu S√∂zlesmenin uygulanmasini kolaylastirmak ve ilgili sahislara bu s√∂zlesmeye g√∂re mevcut hak ve y√ºk√ºml√ºl√ºklerine iliskin hususlarda bilgi vermek amaciyla. √Çkit Taraflarin sigorta kurumlari arasinda irtibat ve bilgi alis verisi saglayan kurum;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p41 ft29"><SPAN class="ft29">(7)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft35">‚ÄúAile Ferdi‚Äù yardimlarin hesabina yapildigi kurumun bulundugu √Çkit Taraf √ºlkesinde y√ºr√ºrl√ºkte bulunan mevzuata g√∂re aile ferdi sayilan kimse;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p42 ft24"><SPAN class="ft24">(8)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft36">‚ÄúIkamet Yeri‚Äù uygulanan mevzuat uyarinca ikamet yeri olarak tanimlanan ya da kabul edilen ikamet yeri;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p43 ft25"><SPAN class="ft25">(9)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft37">‚ÄúSigortalilik S√ºreleri‚Äù hangi mevzuata g√∂re tamamlanmis ise o mevzuatta sigortalilik s√ºreleri olarak taninmis prim √∂deme s√ºreleri, √ßalisma s√ºreleri ve diger kabili kiyas s√ºreler ile belli bir yil veya onun bir kisminda yapilmis olan √ßalisma veya ekonomik faaliyetten dolayi kazanca bagli yaslilik ayligi baglanmasi i√ßin Isve√ß Sosyal Sigorta pl√¢nina g√∂re i√ßinde leyhe aylik puanlarinin veya aylik haklarinin kaydedildigi takvim yillari;</SPAN></P>

<P class="p44 ft23">Bilaga</P>
<P class="p45 ft23"><SPAN class="ft23">(5)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft38">‚ÄúCompetent Insurance Institution‚Äù means the Insurance Institution which is competent under the applicable legislation;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p46 ft25"><SPAN class="ft25">(6)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft37">‚ÄúLiaison body‚Äù means an institution for liaison and information between the insurance institutions of the two Contracting Parties with a view to simplifying the implementation of this Convention and for the information of the persons affected concerning their rights and obligations under the Convention;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p47 ft29"><SPAN class="ft29">(7)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft35">‚ÄúMember of the family‚Äù means a member of the family according to the legislation of the Contracting Party, in whose territory the institution has its seat, at the charge of which the benefits are granted;</SPAN></P>

<P class="p105 ft23">TITLE II</P>
<P class="p106 ft30">Provisions concerning applicable legislation</P>
<P class="p71 ft10">Article 7</P>
<P class="p107 ft33"><SPAN class="ft33">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft44">Save as otherwise provided in Articles 8 and 9, a person being gainfully occupied shall be insured according to the legislation of the Contracting Party in whose territory he is so occupied, regardless of his place of residence or that of his employer.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p108 ft33"><SPAN class="ft33">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft44">Persons who are not gainfully occupied are subject to the legislation of the country in which they reside.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p71 ft10">Article 8</P>
<P class="p109 ft29">1. Where a person, who is insured under the legislation of one Contracting Party and is employed by an employer in the territory of that Party, is sent by that employer to work in the territory of the other Contracting Party, the legislation of the former Party shall continue to apply to him as if he were employed in the territory of that Contracting Party provided that the employment in the territory of the latter Party is not expected to last for more than twelve</P>

<P class="p126 ft29"><SPAN class="ft29">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft41">I fall d√• turkiska arbetstagare √§r underkastade den svenska f√∂rs√§kringslagstiftningen inneb√§r detta f√∂rh√•llande varken hinder mot s√•dana arbetstagares avgiftsbetalning</SPAN></P>

<P class="p37 ft20">Article 16</P>

<P class="p101 ft20">Article 17</P>
<P class="p180 ft29"><SPAN class="ft29">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft41">The Competent Insurance Institution of a Contracting Party shall, when determining the extent to which a person‚Äôs ability to work is lost, apply the legislation to which the Institution itself is subject.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p181 ft29"><SPAN class="ft29">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft41">Medical examinations deemed necessary, shall at the request and expense of the Competent Insurance Institution, be carried out by the Insurance Institution of the place of residence.</SPAN></P>

<P class="p97 ft29">Sayet T√ºrk mevzuatina g√∂re, yardimlardan yararlanma hakki 20nci madde h√ºkm√º uygulanmaksizin kazaniliyorsa, yetkili T√ºrk sigorta kurumu √∂demesi gereken yardim miktarini yalniz kendi mevzuatina g√∂re ge√ßen sigortalilik s√ºrelerini dikkate alarak belirler.</P>

<P class="p205 ft29"><SPAN class="ft29">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft41">In applying Article 21, Swedish periods of insurance are to be taken into account even if they are not regarded as periods of insurance under Turkish legislation.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p206 ft23"><SPAN class="ft23">4.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft45">In computing the amount of pension, only the earnings gained during periods of insurance under Turkish legislation are to be taken into account.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p71 ft10">Article 23</P>
<P class="p207 ft23">If according to Turkish legislation right to benefits exists without any regard being had to article 20, the competent Turkish insurance institution shall calculate the amount of the benefit to be paid with reference only to the insurance periods completed under its own legislation.</P>

<P class="p37 ft23">TITLE IV</P>
<P class="p199 ft10">Miscellaneous Provisions</P>
<P class="p71 ft10">Article 29</P>
<P class="p135 ft26">The supreme administrative authorities may agree on provisions for the implementation of this Convention. Furthermore they shall take steps to ensure that the requisite liaison bodies are set up in the respective territories to facilitate the implementation of this Convention.</P>
<P class="p57 ft10">Article 30</P>
<P class="p135 ft25"><SPAN class="ft25">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft40">For the purpose of applying this Convention, the authorities and institutions of the Contracting Parties shall lend their good offices as though applying their own legislation. Such mutual administrative assistance shall be provided free of charge.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p70 ft29"><SPAN class="ft29">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft41">The correspondence of authorities and institutions, as well as communications from individual persons, may be in Turkish, Swedish, French or English.</SPAN></P>

<DIV id="id_2_3">
<P class="p37 ft10">Article 37</P>
<P class="p207 ft33">1. Disputes arising in connection with the application of this convention are to be resolved by mutual agreement between the supreme administrative authorities of the Contracting Parties.</P>

<P class="p255 ft29"><SPAN class="ft29">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft41">Any benefit which has not been awarded on account of the nationality of the person concerned or which has been withdrawn on account of his residence in the territory of the other Contracting Party shall, upon application, be awarded or resumed with effect from the date of entry into force of this Convention.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p256 ft26"><SPAN class="ft26">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft43">Upon application being received, a benefit granted prior to the entry into force of this Convention shall be recalculated in compliance with the provisions of the same. Such benefits may also be recalculated without any application being made. This recalculation may not result in any reduction of the benefit paid.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p257 ft29"><SPAN class="ft29">4.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft41">Provisions in the legislations of the Contracting Parties concerning prescription and the termination of the right to benefits shall not apply to rights arising out of the provisions of paragraphs (1)‚Äì</SPAN></P>
<P class="p258 ft23"><SPAN class="ft23">(3)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft38">of this Article, always provided that the beneficiary submits his application for benefit within two years after the date of entry into force of this Convention.</SPAN></P>

<P class="p37 ft10">Artikel 12</P>
<P class="p357 ft20"><SPAN class="ft20">a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft32">Denna till√§ggskonvention tr√§der i kraft den f√∂rsta dagen i den tredje m√•naden efter den m√•nad d√• regeringarna fr√•n varandra har mottagit skriftligt meddelande om att alla de konstitutionella formaliteterna f√∂r denna till√§ggskonventions ikrafttr√§dande har uppfyllts.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p358 ft24"><SPAN class="ft24">b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft42">Till√§mpningen av denna till√§ggskonvention skall inte f√∂ranleda minskning av f√∂rm√•nsbelopp som en person har beviljats f√∂re ikrafttr√§dandet.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p359 ft25"><SPAN class="ft25">c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft40">Konventionen och till√§ggs√∂verenskommelsen enligt deras lydelser f√∂re denna till√§ggskonventions ikraftr√§dande skall forts√§tta att g√§lla med avseende p√• r√§tt till f√∂rm√•ner som kan fastst√§llas genom till√§mpning av konventionen och till√§ggs√∂verenskommelsen i deras lydelser f√∂re denna till√§ggskonventions ikrafttr√§dande.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p143 ft23"><SPAN class="ft23">d)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft45">Denna till√§ggskonvention skall f√∂rbli i kraft under samma tid som konventionen och till√§ggs√∂verenskommelsen.</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2">
<P class="p360 ft24">akdolunan Sosyal G√ºvenlik S√∂zlesmesi‚Äône iliskin olup, 30.06.1978 tarihinde imzalanan Protokol y√ºr√ºrl√ºkten kaldirilmistir.</P>
<P class="p71 ft10">Madde 12</P>
<P class="p361 ft23"><SPAN class="ft23">a.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft45">Bu Ek S√∂zlesme, her bir H√ºk√ºmet‚Äôin, bu Ek S√∂zlesme‚Äônin y√ºr√ºrl√ºge girmesi i√ßin b√ºt√ºn yasal ve Anayasal gerekliliklerin yerine getirildigini belirten yazili bildirimi diger H√ºk√ºmet‚Äôten aldigi ayi izleyen √º√ß√ºnc√º ayin birinci g√ºn√º y√ºr√ºrl√ºge girer.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p362 ft33"><SPAN class="ft33">b.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft44">Bu Ek S√∂zlesme‚Äônin uygulanmasi, y√ºr√ºrl√ºge girmesinden √∂nce hak kazanilmis olan bir yardimin tutarinda herhangi bir indirim yapilmasi sonucunu dogurmaz.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p81 ft25"><SPAN class="ft25">c.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft40">Bu Ek S√∂zlesme‚Äônin y√ºr√ºrl√ºge girmesinden √∂nce y√ºr√ºrl√ºkte olan S√∂zlesme ve Ek Anlasma, bu Ek S√∂zlesme‚Äônin y√ºr√ºrl√ºge girmesinden √∂nce y√ºr√ºrl√ºkte olan S√∂zlesme‚Äônin ve Ek Anlasma‚Äônin uygulanmasi ile kazanilmasi m√ºmk√ºn olabilen yardim haklari y√∂n√ºnden uygulanmaya devam olunur.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p363 ft24"><SPAN class="ft24">d.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft42">Bu Ek S√∂zlesme, S√∂zlesme ve Ek Anlasma ile ayni s√ºrece y√ºr√ºrl√ºkte kalir.</SPAN></P>

<P class="p44 ft30">Prop. 2004/05:71</P>
<P class="p44 ft29">Bilaga</P>
<P class="p364 ft23">Kingdom of Sweden and the Republic of Turkey on Social Security signed 30 June 1978 at Stockholm shall be abolished.</P>
<P class="p41 ft10">Article 12</P>
<P class="p365 ft25"><SPAN class="ft25">a.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft40">This Supplementary Convention shall enter into force on the first day of the third month following the month in which each Government shall have received from the other Government written notification that it has complied with all statutory and constitutional requirements for the entry into force of this Supplementary Convention.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p366 ft20"><SPAN class="ft20">b.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft32">The application of this Supplementary Convention shall not result in any reduction in the amount of a benefit to which entitlement was established prior to its entry into force.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p367 ft20"><SPAN class="ft20">c.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft32">The Convention and the Supplementary Agreement as in force prior to the entry into force of this Supplementary Convention shall continue to apply in regard to rights to benefits which can be established through the application of the Convention and the Supplementary Agreement as in force prior to the entry into force of this Supplementary Convention.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p368 ft24"><SPAN class="ft24">d.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft42">This Supplementary Convention shall remain in force for the same period as the Convention and the Supplementary Agreement.</SPAN></P>
